***smous.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:smous.html>smous</a> (50695)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">משה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">moyshe</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Moses</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, pronounced <i>moushe</i> in Western Yiddish, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">מֹשֶׁה</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">moshé</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Moses</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smous.html>smous</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smous.html>smousen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">smouzen</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smous.html>smousje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ethnic slur<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">Jew</span> <span class="defdate">[from mid 17th c.]</span></li>
<li>A small breed of terrier with a light to dark <a href = vnd.unilang:beige.html>beige</a> fur, native to the Netherlands. <span class="defdate">[from mid 19th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1848</b> May 11, Advertisement 7018, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:algemeen.html>Algemeen</a> Handelsblad</i>, No. 5136, page 4.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vermist.html>Vermist</a> :</b> Den 9den <a href = vnd.unilang:mei.html>Mei</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kleine.html>Kleine</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jonge.html>Jonge</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>Hond</a>,</b> Poesbaard of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:smous.html>Smousje</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kleur.html>kleur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lichtbruin.html>Lichtbruin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> eenig <a href = vnd.unilang:zwart.html>Zwart</a> doorgeslagen, <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hals.html>hals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderste.html>onderste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedeelte.html>gedeelte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a> pooten <a href = vnd.unilang:wit.html>wit</a>,<a href = vnd.unilang:luisterende.html>luisterende</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:naam.html>naam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b>DJALMA.</b></span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">MISSING: The 9th of <a href = vnd.unilang:mai.html>Mai</a>, one SMALL YOUNG DOG, "Cat beard" or <b>little <a href = vnd.unilang:smous.html>Smous</a></b> (indication of breed), color: Light Brown with some Black coming through, the front of the neck and the down part of the four <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a> White, listens to the name DJALMA.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">smoushond</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:smurf.html>smurf</a> (37751)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Changed from the original <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">schtroumpf</i> as described above.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smurf.html>smurf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smurfen.html>smurfen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smurf.html>smurfje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>Possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">snake</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:joker.html>joker</a>, prankster</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possible etymologically the same as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">snake</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:viper.html>viper</a>, snake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (see more at English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">snake</i>). Possibly related to Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snakken.html>snakken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to talk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:snacken.html>snacken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*snakkon</i>. Related to Swedish <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">snacka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to talk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and Low German <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:snacken.html>snacken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to talk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the sense of "to open the mouth".

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuw.html>sneeuw</a> (2412)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">snêe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">snēo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*snaiwaz</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sneuwen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuwen.html>sneeuwen</a></i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuw.html>sneeuw</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>. Displaced Middle Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">snuwen</i> due to analogy with <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:regenen.html>regenen</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hagelen.html>hagelen</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick, fast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:snel.html>snel</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lively, quick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*snellaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">active, swift, brisk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx"><a href = vnd.unilang:snel.html>snel</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">active, strenuous</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snel.html>snel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:snel.html>snel</a></i> (whence German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:schnell.html>schnell</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick, swift</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">שנעל</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">shnel</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick, swift</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">snello</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick, nimble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">esnel, isnel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Occitan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Occitan language">Occitan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="oc">isnel, irnel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">snjallr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">skilful, excellent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (whence Danish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">snild</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clever</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sneller.html>sneller</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">snellest</b>)
</p><p><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now chiefly  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>Quick, smart; sharp, active, brisk or nimble; lively.
<ul><li><b>1720</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Allan Ramsay, <i>Edinburgh's Salutation to Lord Carnarvon</i>.
<dl><dd>That in ilk action, wise and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></b> / You may shaw Manly fire.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1852</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> John Brown, "<a href = vnd.unilang:rab.html>Rab</a> and his Friends".
<dl><dd>That horny-handed, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></b>, peremptory little <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1889</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> James Robertson, <i>The Early Religion of Israel</i>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:amos.html>Amos</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a lithe, keen, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Quick-witted; witty.</li>
<li>Harsh; severe.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">snelly</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">snells</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A short line of horsehair, gut, <a href = vnd.unilang:monofilament.html>monofilament</a>, etc., by which a fishhook or lure <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> attached to a longer (and usually heavier) line.
<ul><li><b>1979</b>, Cormac McCarthy, <i>Suttree</i>, Random House, p.194:
<dl><dd>He tied on new baited <b>snells</b> and recovered the current with the oars.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a> knot</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">snells</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">snelling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">snelled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To tie a hook to the end of a fishing line with a <a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a> knot.
<dl><dd><i>Can you show <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> how to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snell.html>snell</a></b> a hook?</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr />
</body>

***sneltrein.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sneltrein.html>sneltrein</a> (33817)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snel.html>snel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trein.html>trein</a></i>.

***snicker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snicker.html>snicker</a> (88079)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>US variant of the British <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">snigger</i>, possibly of imitative origin, similar to Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snikken.html>snikken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to gasp; sob</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The noun <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> first recorded 1836, from the verb. Compare also Scottish <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">smicker</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to smile or laugh in a sniggering or <a href = vnd.unilang:leery.html>leery</a> way, smirk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">smicker</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snicker.html>snicker</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snickers.html>snickers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A stifled or broken laugh.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snicker.html>snicker</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snickers.html>snickers</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">snickering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">snickered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To emit a <a href = vnd.unilang:snicker.html>snicker</a>, a stifled or broken laugh.
<ul><li><b>1915</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/T.S._Eliot" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:T.S. Eliot"><a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>.S. Eliot</a>, "The Love Song of J. Alfred Prufrock":
<dl><dd>I have seen the eternal Footman hold my coat, and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:snicker.html>snicker</a></b> <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To utter through a laugh of this <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a horse</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To whinny.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>See also Thesaurus:laugh</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">snick</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snicker.html>snicker</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snickers.html>snickers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cricket<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A player who snicks the ball.</li></ol>
</body>

***snijboon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snijboon.html>snijboon</a> (67426)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snijden.html>snijden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">boon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bean</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, named because they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> usually cut into small pieces before cooking or eating.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snijboon.html>snijboon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snijbonen.html>snijbonen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snijboon.html>snijboontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> bean</span>, a long variety of <i>Phaseolus <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></i>, with <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> pods and fully matured seeds.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sniden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">snīthan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*snīþaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sneyt-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***snikken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snikken.html>snikken</a> (34676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">snicken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sob; gasp for breath</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  Probably related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snuiven.html>snuiven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sniff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> under the influence of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snakken.html>snakken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to open the mouth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hik.html>hik</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hiccup</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">snucken</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">snokke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sob</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Norwegian dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">snukka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sniff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, German dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schnuckeln</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schnauken</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schnäuken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sniff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, English dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">snock</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sniff; sob forcefully</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snikken.html>snikken</a></strong>

***snip.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:snip.html>snip</a> (99670)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">snippe</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snip.html>snip</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snippen.html>snippen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:snip.html>snipje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A snipe or <a href = vnd.unilang:woodcock.html>woodcock</a>, thin-beaked bird of the genera <i>Gallinago</i>, <i>Scolopax</i>, <i>Lymnocryptes</i>, <i>Limnodromus</i> and <i>Coenocorypha</i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A 100 guilders banknote.</li></ol>
